     <pre><code>// Exercise: Build a robust form validation system\nclass FormValidator {\n    constructor(schema) {\n        this.schema = schema;\n        this.errors = {};\n    }\n    \n    validate(data) {\n        this.errors = {};\n        \n        for (const [field, rules] of Object.entries(this.schema)) {\n            const value = data[field];\n            \n            // Required check\n            if (rules.required && this.isEmpty(value)) {\n                this.addError(field, `${this.formatFieldName(field)} is required`);\n                continue;\n            }\n            \n            // Skip other validations if empty and not required\n            if (this.isEmpty(value) && !rules.required) continue;\n            \n            // Type validation\n            if (rules.type && !this.checkType(value, rules.type)) {\n                this.addError(field, `${this.formatFieldName(field)} must be a ${rules.type}`);\n            }\n            \n            // Custom validators\n            if (rules.validators) {\n                for (const validator of rules.validators) {\n                    const result = validator(value, data);\n                    if (result !== true) {\n                        this.addError(field, result);\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return Object.keys(this.errors).length === 0;\n    }\n    \n    isEmpty(value) {\n        return value === undefined || value === null || value === "";\n    }\n    \n    checkType(value, type) {\n        switch (type) {\n            case "string": return typeof value === "string";\n            case "number": return typeof value === "number" && !isNaN(value);\n            case "boolean": return typeof value === "boolean";\n            case "array": return Array.isArray(value);\n            case "email": return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(value);\n            default: return true;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    addError(field, message) {\n        if (!this.errors[field]) {\n            this.errors[field] = [];\n        }\n        this.errors[field].push(message);\n    }\n    \n    formatFieldName(field) {\n        return field.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + field.slice(1).replace(/([A-Z])/g, \' $1\');\n    }\n    \n    getErrors() {\n        return this.errors;\n    }\n    \n    hasErrors() {\n        return Object.keys(this.errors).length > 0;\n    }\n}\n\n// Define schema and use\nconst registrationSchema = {\n    email: {\n        type: "email",\n        required: true\n    },\n    password: {\n        type: "string",\n        required: true,\n        validators: [\n            (value) => value.length >= 8 || "Password must be at least 8 characters",\n            (value) => /[A-Z]/.test(value) || "Password must contain an uppercase letter",\n            (value) => /[0-9]/.test(value) || "Password must contain a number"\n        ]\n    },\n    confirmPassword: {\n        required: true,\n        validators: [\n            (value, data) => value === data.password || "Passwords do not match"\n        ]\n    },\n    age: {\n        type: "number",\n        required: false,\n        validators: [\n            (value) => value >= 18 || "Must be at least 18 years old"\n        ]\n    }\n};\n\nconst validator = new FormValidator(registrationSchema);\n\nconst formData = {\n    email: "invalid-email",\n    password: "short",\n    confirmPassword: "different",\n    age: 16\n};\n\nif (!validator.validate(formData)) {\n    console.log("Validation errors:", validator.getErrors());\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <div class="navigation-buttons">\n                <a This allows web applications to remember user preferences, save progress, cache data for offline use, and provide a better user experience. The main storage options are localStorage, sessionStorage, cookies, and IndexedDB, each with different use cases and limitations.</p>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Key Concept:</strong> localStorage persists indefinitely, sessionStorage lasts only for the session (until tab closes), cookies are sent to the server with requests, and IndexedDB is for large amounts of structured data.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>localStorage Basics</h2>\n                <p>Store data that persists across browser sessions:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Store data\nlocalStorage.setItem("username", "john_doe");\nlocalStorage.setItem("theme", "dark");\nlocalStorage.setItem("language", "en");\n\n// Retrieve data\nconst username = localStorage.getItem("username");\nconsole.log(username);  // "john_doe"\n\n// Get non-existent key\nconst missing = localStorage.getItem("nonexistent");\nconsole.log(missing);  // null\n\n// Remove specific item\nlocalStorage.removeItem("theme");\n\n// Clear all storage\nlocalStorage.clear();\n\n// Check if key exists\nif (localStorage.getItem("username") !== null) {\n    console.log("Username exists");\n}\n\n// Get number of items stored\nconst count = localStorage.length;\nconsole.log(`Storage has ${count} items`);</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <strong>localStorage Methods:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><code>setItem(key, value)</code> - Store a value (must be string)</li>\n                        <li><code>getItem(key)</code> - Retrieve a value (returns null if not found)</li>\n                        <li><code>removeItem(key)</code> - Delete a specific item</li>\n                        <li><code>clear()</code> - Delete all stored data</li>\n                        <li><code>length</code> - Number of items stored</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n\n                <h3>Dot Notation and Property Access</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Alternative syntax (not recommended)\nlocalStorage.username = "john_doe";\nconsole.log(localStorage.username);  // "john_doe"\ndelete localStorage.username;\n\n// Why prefer setItem/getItem:\nlocalStorage.setItem("setItem", "works");\nlocalStorage.setItem("length", "custom value");  // Works\n\nlocalStorage.length = "custom";  // Doesn\'t work! \n// length is a read-only property\n\n// Iterating over storage\nfor (let i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++) {\n    const key = localStorage.key(i);\n    const value = localStorage.getItem(key);\n    console.log(`${key}: ${value}`);\n}\n\n// Using Object methods\nconst keys = Object.keys(localStorage);\nconst values = Object.values(localStorage);\nconst entries = Object.entries(localStorage);</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Storing Complex Data</h2>\n                <p>localStorage only stores strings, so we need JSON for objects and arrays:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Storing objects\nconst user = {\n    name: "Alice",\n    email: "alice@example.com",\n    preferences: {\n        theme: "dark",\n        notifications: true\n    }\n};\n\n// Convert to JSON string before storing\nlocalStorage.setItem("user", JSON.stringify(user));\n\n// Parse when retrieving\nconst storedUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"));\nconsole.log(storedUser.name); JSON.parse(value) : defaultValue;\n    } catch (error) {\n        console.error(`Error parsing ${key}:`, error);\n        return defaultValue;\n    }\n}\n\nconst settings = getJSON("settings", { theme: "light" });\n\n// Updating stored objects\nfunction updateUser(updates) {\n    const user = getJSON("user", {});\n    const updated = { ...user, ...updates };\n    localStorage.setItem("user", JSON.stringify(updated));\n    return updated;\n}\n\nupdateUser({ name: "Alice Smith" });</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>sessionStorage</h2>\n                <p>Storage that only lasts for the current session:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Same API as localStorage\nsessionStorage.setItem("tempData", "cleared on tab close");\nconst data = sessionStorage.getItem("tempData");\nsessionStorage.removeItem("tempData");\nsessionStorage.clear();\n\n// Use cases for sessionStorage\n// 1. Form data being filled (survives page refresh)\nsessionStorage.setItem("formData", JSON.stringify({\n    name: "John",\n    email: "john@example.com"\n}));\n\n// 2. Temporary state\nsessionStorage.setItem("redirectAfterLogin", "/dashboard");\n\n// 3. One-time notifications\nsessionStorage.setItem("showWelcome", "true");\n\n// Difference from localStorage\n// localStorage: Data persists until cleared\n// sessionStorage: Data clears when tab/window closes\n\n// Check storage type\nconst isLocalStorage = typeof localStorage !== "undefined";\nconst isSessionStorage = typeof sessionStorage !== "undefined";</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <strong>When to Use Which:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><strong>localStorage:</strong> User preferences, theme, cached data, remember login</li>\n                        <li><strong>sessionStorage:</strong> Form data, temporary state, one-time messages, multi-step wizard</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Storage Events</h2>\n                <p>Listen for changes in other tabs/windows:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Listen for storage changes from other tabs\nwindow.addEventListener("storage", (event) => {\n    console.log("Key changed:", event.key);\n    console.log("Old value:", event.oldValue);\n    console.log("New value:", event.newValue);\n    console.log("URL:", event.url);\n    \n    // React to changes\n    if (event.key === "theme") {\n        applyTheme(event.newValue);\n    }\n    \n    if (event.key === "logout") {\n        // Another tab logged out\n        window.location.href = "/login";\n    }\n});\n\n// Example: Sync theme across tabs\nfunction setTheme(theme) {\n    localStorage.setItem("theme", theme);\n    applyTheme(theme);\n}\n\nfunction applyTheme(theme) {\n    document.body.className = theme;\n}\n\n// Initialize from storage\nconst savedTheme = localStorage.getItem("theme") || "light";\napplyTheme(savedTheme);\n\n// Example: Broadcast logout\nfunction logout() {\n    localStorage.removeItem("token");\n    localStorage.setItem("logout", Date.now().toString());\n    window.location.href = "/login";\n}\n\n// Example: Tab communication\nfunction sendMessage(message) {\n    localStorage.setItem("message", JSON.stringify({\n        ...message,\n        timestamp: }\n});</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Important:</strong> The storage event only fires in OTHER tabs/windows, not in the tab that made the change. This is useful for syncing state across tabs.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Storage Limits and Quotas</h2>\n                <p>Understand browser storage limitations:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Typical storage limit: 5-10 MB per origin\n// localStorage and sessionStorage share this limit\n\n// Check available storage (not universally supported)\nif (navigator.storage && navigator.storage.estimate) {\n    navigator.storage.estimate().then(({ quota, usage }) => {\n        console.log(`Used: ${usage} bytes`);\n        console.log(`Available: ${quota} bytes`);\n        console.log(`Used: ${(usage / quota * 100).toFixed(2)}%`);\n    });\n}\n\n// Handle quota exceeded error\nfunction safeSetItem(key, value) {\n    try {\n        localStorage.setItem(key, value);\n        return true;\n    } catch (error) {\n        if (error.name === "QuotaExceededError") {\n            console.error("Storage quota exceeded");\n            // Option 1: Clear old data\n            clearOldData();\n            // Option 2: Ask user\n            alert("Storage full. Please clear some data.");\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n}\n\n// Estimate size of data\nfunction getStringSize(str) {\n    return new Blob([str]).size;\n}\n\nconst data = JSON.stringify({ large: "object" });\nconsole.log(`Size: ${getStringSize(data)} bytes`);\n\n// Manage storage efficiently\nclass StorageManager {\n    constructor(prefix = "app_") {\n        this.prefix = prefix;\n    }\n    \n    set(key, value, ttl = null) {\n        const data = {\n            value,\n            timestamp: Date.now(),\n            ttl\n        };\n        \n        try {\n            localStorage.setItem(\n                this.prefix + key,\n                JSON.stringify(data)\n            );\n            return true;\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error("Storage error:", error);\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    get(key) {\n        const raw = localStorage.getItem(this.prefix + key);\n        if (!raw) return null;\n        \n        try {\n            const data = JSON.parse(raw);\n            \n            // Check TTL\n            if (data.ttl && Date.now() > data.timestamp + data.ttl) {\n                this.remove(key);\n                return null;\n            }\n            \n            return data.value;\n        } catch {\n            return null;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    remove(key) {\n        localStorage.removeItem(this.prefix + key);\n    }\n    \n    clear() {\n        const keys = Object.keys(localStorage)\n            .filter(k => k.startsWith(this.prefix));\n        keys.forEach(k => localStorage.removeItem(k));\n    }\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Practical Patterns</h2>\n                <p>Common patterns for using localStorage effectively:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Pattern 1: User Preferences\nconst preferences = {\n    get(key, defaultValue = null) {\n        const prefs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("preferences") || "{}");\n        return prefs[key] ?? defaultValue;\n    },\n    \n    set(key, value) {\n        const prefs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("preferences") || "{}");\n        prefs[key] = value;\n        localStorage.setItem("preferences", JSON.stringify(prefs));\n    },\n    \n    remove(key) {\n        const prefs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("preferences") || "{}");\n        delete prefs[key];\n        localStorage.setItem("preferences", JSON.stringify(prefs));\n    }\n};\n\npreferences.set("theme", "dark");\npreferences.set("fontSize", 16);\nconsole.log(preferences.get("theme"));  // "dark"\n\n// Pattern 2: Offline Data Cache\nclass OfflineCache {\n    constructor(name, ttl = 3600000) {  // Default 1 hour\n        this.name = name;\n        this.ttl = ttl;\n    }\n    \n    async get(key, fetcher) {\n        const cacheKey = `${this.name}_${key}`;\n        const cached = this.getFromCache(cacheKey);\n        \n        if (cached) return cached;\n        \n        const data = await fetcher();\n        this.setToCache(cacheKey, data);\n        return data;\n    }\n    \n    getFromCache(key) {\n        const raw = localStorage.getItem(key);\n        if (!raw) return null;\n        \n        const { data, timestamp } = JSON.parse(raw);\n        \n        if (Date.now() - timestamp > this.ttl) {\n            localStorage.removeItem(key);\n            return null;\n        }\n        \n        return data;\n    }\n    \n    setToCache(key, data) {\n        localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify({\n            data,\n            timestamp: Date.now()\n        }));\n    }\n    \n    invalidate(key) {\n        localStorage.removeItem(`${this.name}_${key}`);\n    }\n}\n\n// Usage\nconst userCache = new OfflineCache("users", 300000);  // 5 minutes\nconst user = await userCache.get("user_123", () => \n    fetch("/api/users/123").then(r => r.json())\n);\n\n// Pattern 3: Form State Persistence\nclass FormState {\n    constructor(formId, fields) {\n        this.formId = formId;\n        this.fields = fields;\n        this.key = `form_${formId}`;\n    }\n    \n    save() {\n        const state = {};\n        this.fields.forEach(field => {\n            const input = document.querySelector(`[name="${field}"]`);\n            if (input) state[field] = input.value;\n        });\n        localStorage.setItem(this.key, JSON.stringify(state));\n    }\n    \n    restore() {\n        const state = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.key) || "{}");\n        this.fields.forEach(field => {\n            const input = document.querySelector(`[name="${field}"]`);\n            if (input && state[field]) {\n                input.value = state[field];\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    \n    clear() {\n        localStorage.removeItem(this.key);\n    }\n}\n\n// Auto-save form\nconst formState = new FormState("registration", ["name", "email", "phone"]);\nformState.restore();\n\ndocument.querySelector("#registration").addEventListener("input", \n    debounce(() => formState.save(), 500)\n);</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Cookies</h2>\n                <p>Another way to store data, sent to the server:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Setting cookies\ndocument.cookie = "username=john_doe";\ndocument.cookie = "theme=dark";\ndocument.cookie = "session_id=abc123; path=/";\n\n// Cookie with expiration\nconst days = 7;\nconst date = new Date();\ndate.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));\ndocument.cookie = `remember_me=true; expires=${date.toUTCString()}; path=/`;\n\n// Reading cookies\nfunction getCookie(name) {\n    const cookies = document.cookie.split("; ");\n    for (const cookie of cookies) {\n        const [key, value] = cookie.split("=");\n        if (key === name) return decodeURIComponent(value);\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\nconsole.log(getCookie("username"));  // "john_doe"\n\n// Deleting cookies\nfunction deleteCookie(name) {\n    document.cookie = `${name}=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;`;\n}\n\n// Cookie helper library\nconst cookies = {\n    set(name, value, options = {}) {\n        let cookie = `${encodeURIComponent(name)}=${encodeURIComponent(value)}`;\n        \n        if (options.days) {\n            const date = new Date();\n            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (options.days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));\n            cookie += `; expires=${date.toUTCString()}`;\n        }\n        \n        if (options.path) cookie += `; path=${options.path}`;\n        if (options.domain) cookie += `; domain=${options.domain}`;\n        if (options.secure) cookie += "; secure";\n        if (options.httpOnly) cookie += "; HttpOnly";\n        if (options.sameSite) cookie += `; SameSite=${options.sameSite}`;\n        \n        document.cookie = cookie;\n    },\n    \n    get(name) {\n        return getCookie(name);\n    },\n    \n    remove(name, options = {}) {\n        let cookie = `${name}=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC`;\n        if (options.path) cookie += `; path=${options.path}`;\n        document.cookie = cookie;\n    }\n};\n\n// Usage\ncookies.set("token", "abc123", { days: 30, secure: true, sameSite: "Strict" });</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="code-explanation">\n                    <strong>localStorage vs Cookies:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><strong>Cookies:</strong> Sent to server with every request, smaller limit (4KB), good for auth</li>\n                        <li><strong>localStorage:</strong> Not sent to server, larger limit (5MB+), good for client data</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>IndexedDB Overview</h2>\n                <p>For large amounts of structured data:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// IndexedDB is a full database in the browser\n// Much more powerful but more complex than localStorage\n\n// Simple wrapper for IndexedDB\nclass SimpleDB {\n    constructor(dbName, storeName, version = 1) {\n        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n            const request = indexedDB.open(dbName, version);\n            \n            request.onerror = () => reject(request.error);\n            \n            request.onsuccess = () => {\n                this.db = request.result;\n                this.storeName = storeName;\n                resolve(this);\n            };\n            \n            request.onupgradeneeded = (event) => {\n                const db = event.target.result;\n                if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(storeName)) {\n                    db.createObjectStore(storeName, { keyPath: "id" });\n                }\n            };\n        });\n    }\n    \n    async add(data) {\n        return this.transaction("readwrite", (store) => \n            this.promisify(store.add(data))\n        );\n    }\n    \n    async get(id) {\n        return this.transaction("readonly", (store) => \n            this.promisify(store.get(id))\n        );\n    }\n    \n    async put(data) {\n        return this.transaction("readwrite", (store) => \n            this.promisify(store.put(data))\n        );\n    }\n    \n    async delete(id) {\n        return this.transaction("readwrite", (store) => \n            this.promisify(store.delete(id))\n        );\n    }\n    \n    async getAll() {\n        return this.transaction("readonly", (store) => \n            this.promisify(store.getAll())\n        );\n    }\n    \n    async transaction(mode, operation) {\n        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n            const transaction = this.db.transaction(this.storeName, mode);\n            const store = transaction.objectStore(this.storeName);\n            const request = operation(store);\n            \n            request.onsuccess = () => resolve(request.result);\n            request.onerror = () => reject(request.error);\n        });\n    }\n    \n    promisify(request) {\n        return request;  // Handled by transaction wrapper\n    }\n}\n\n// Usage\nconst db = await new SimpleDB("MyApp", "users");\nawait db.add({ id: 1, name: "Alice", email: "alice@example.com" });\nconst user = await db.get(1);\nconsole.log(user);\nconst allUsers = await db.getAll();\n\n// When to use IndexedDB:\n// - Large datasets (100MB+)\n// - Complex queries and indexes\n// - Offline-first applications\n// - Storing files or blobs</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Security Considerations</h2>\n                <p>Keep stored data safe:</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// DON\'T store sensitive data in localStorage\n// ❌ Bad - passwords, tokens, personal info\nlocalStorage.setItem("password", "secret123");  // NEVER!\n\n// Anyone with access to the computer can read this\n// XSS attacks can steal this data\n\n// If you must store tokens, use secure patterns\n// Option 1: HttpOnly cookies (server sets)\n// Option 2: Short-lived tokens with refresh\n// Option 3: Encrypt sensitive data\n\n// Simple encryption helper (not cryptographically secure)\nfunction encrypt(text, key) {\n    return btoa(encodeURIComponent(text));\n}\n\nfunction decrypt(encoded, key) {\n    return decodeURIComponent(atob(encoded));\n}\n\n// For real encryption, use Web Crypto API\nasync function encryptData(data, password) {\n    const encoder = new TextEncoder();\n    const dataBuffer = encoder.encode(JSON.stringify(data));\n    \n    const keyMaterial = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\n        "raw",\n        encoder.encode(password),\n        { name: "PBKDF2" },\n        false,\n        ["deriveKey"]\n    );\n    \n    const key = await crypto.subtle.deriveKey(\n        { name: "PBKDF2", salt: encoder.encode("salt"), iterations: 100000, hash: "SHA-256" },\n        keyMaterial,\n        { name: "AES-GCM", length: 256 },\n        false,\n        ["encrypt"]\n    );\n    \n    const iv = crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(12));\n    const encrypted = await crypto.subtle.encrypt(\n        { name: "AES-GCM", iv },\n        key,\n        dataBuffer\n    );\n    \n    return { iv: Array.from(iv), data: Array.from(new Uint8Array(encrypted)) };\n}\n\n// Clear sensitive data on logout\nfunction logout() {\n    // Clear all storage\n    localStorage.clear();\n    sessionStorage.clear();\n    \n    // Clear specific items\n    localStorage.removeItem("token");\n    localStorage.removeItem("user");\n    \n    // Redirect\n    window.location.href = "/login";\n}\n\n// Validate stored data\nfunction getValidatedUser() {\n    const raw = localStorage.getItem("user");\n    if (!raw) return null;\n    \n    try {\n        const user = JSON.parse(raw);\n        \n        // Validate structure\n        if (typeof user.id !== "number" || typeof user.name !== "string") {\n            localStorage.removeItem("user");\n            return null;\n        }\n        \n        return user;\n    } catch {\n        localStorage.removeItem("user");\n        return null;\n    }\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <section class="content-section">\n                <h2>Practice Exercise</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>// Exercise: Build a complete storage manager\nclass StorageService {\n    constructor(namespace = "app") {\n        this.namespace = namespace;\n        this.cache = new Map();\n    }\n    \n    // Prefix keys with namespace\n    prefix(key) {\n        return `${this.namespace}_${key}`;\n    }\n    \n    // Store with optional TTL\n    set(key, value, ttlMs = null) {\n        const data = {\n            value,\n            meta: {\n                created: Date.now(),\n                ttl: ttlMs\n            }\n        };\n        \n        try {\n            const serialized = JSON.stringify(data);\n            localStorage.setItem(this.prefix(key), serialized);\n            this.cache.set(key, data);\n            return true;\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error("Storage error:", error);\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Retrieve with TTL check\n    get(key, defaultValue = null) {\n        // Check memory cache first\n        if (this.cache.has(key)) {\n            const cached = this.cache.get(key);\n            if (!this.isExpired(cached)) {\n                return cached.value;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Check localStorage\n        const raw = localStorage.getItem(this.prefix(key));\n        if (!raw) return defaultValue;\n        \n        try {\n            const data = JSON.parse(raw);\n            \n            if (this.isExpired(data)) {\n                this.remove(key);\n                return defaultValue;\n            }\n            \n            this.cache.set(key, data);\n            return data.value;\n        } catch {\n            return defaultValue;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Check if data is expired\n    isExpired(data) {\n        if (!data.meta?.ttl) return false;\n        return Date.now() > data.meta.created + data.meta.ttl;\n    }\n    \n    // Remove item\n    remove(key) {\n        localStorage.removeItem(this.prefix(key));\n        this.cache.delete(key);\n    }\n    \n    // Clear all items in namespace\n    clearAll() {\n        const keys = Object.keys(localStorage)\n            .filter(k => k.startsWith(this.namespace + "_"));\n        \n        keys.forEach(k => {\n            localStorage.removeItem(k);\n            this.cache.delete(k.replace(this.namespace + "_", ""));\n        });\n    }\n    \n    // Get all keys in namespace\n    keys() {\n        return Object.keys(localStorage)\n            .filter(k => k.startsWith(this.namespace + "_"))\n            .map(k => k.replace(this.namespace + "_", ""));\n    }\n    \n    // Export all data\n    export() {\n        const data = {};\n        this.keys().forEach(key => {\n            data[key] = this.get(key);\n        });\n        return data;\n    }\n    \n    // Import data\n    import(data) {\n        Object.entries(data).forEach(([key, value]) => {\n            this.set(key, value);\n        });\n    }\n}\n\n// Use it\nconst storage = new StorageService("myApp");\n\n// Store user preferences\nstorage.set("preferences", {\n    theme: "dark",\n    language: "en",\n    notifications: true\n});\n\n// Store with expiration (1 hour)\nstorage.set("session_token", "abc123", 3600000);\n\n// Retrieve\nconst prefs = storage.get("preferences");\nconsole.log(prefs);\n\n// Create a todo list using storage\nclass TodoList {\n    constructor(storage) {\n        this.storage = storage;\n        this.todos = this.storage.get("todos", []);\n    }\n    \n    add(text) {\n        const todo = {\n            id: Date.now(),\n            text,\n            done: false,\n            created: new Date().toISOString()\n        };\n        this.todos.push(todo);\n        this.save();\n        return todo;\n    }\n    \n    toggle(id) {\n        const todo = this.todos.find(t => t.id === id);\n        if (todo) {\n            todo.done = !todo.done;\n            this.save();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    remove(id) {\n        this.todos = this.todos.filter(t => t.id !== id);\n        this.save();\n    }\n    \n    save() {\n        this.storage.set("todos", this.todos);\n    }\n    \n    getAll() {\n        return this.todos;\n    }\n    \n    getActive() {\n        return this.todos.filter(t => !t.done);\n    }\n    \n    getCompleted() {\n        return this.todos.filter(t => t.done);\n    }\n}\n\nconst todoStorage = new StorageService("todos");\nconst todos = new TodoList(todoStorage);\ntodos.add("Learn localStorage");\ntodos.add("Build a project");\nconsole.log(todos.getAll());</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n\n            <div
